In [87]:



    


sentiment_dict = {}
label_dict = {}

for topic in topic_nums:
    current_list = []
    current_list_label = []
    documents, doc_scores, doc_ids = model.search_documents_by_topic(topic_num=topic, num_docs=1000, reduced=True)
    for i, document in enumerate(documents):
        try:
            labels = classifier(document)[0]['label']
            scores = classifier(document)[0]['score']
            current_list.append(scores)
            current_list_label.append(labels)
        except Exception as e:
            print(e)
    sentiment_dict[str(topic)] = current_list
    label_dict[str(topic)] = current_list_label
